<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-indent: 0.5in">&#160;</p>

issued a press release announcing its unaudited financial results for the quarter ended March 31, 2024. A copy of the press release making
the announcement is attached as Exhibit 99.1 to this Current Report on Form 8-K and is incorporated herein by reference.</p>

<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: right; background-color: white"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>IT Tech Packaging,
Inc. Announces First Quarter 2024 Unaudited Financial Results</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">BAODING,&nbsp;China,&nbsp;May
10, 2024&nbsp;/PRNewswire/ --&nbsp;IT Tech Packaging, Inc. (NYSE American: ITP) (&ldquo;IT Tech Packaging&rdquo; or the &ldquo;Company&rdquo;),
a leading manufacturer and distributor of diversified paper products in&nbsp;North China, today announced its unaudited financial results
for the first&nbsp;quarter ended&nbsp;March 31, 2024.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Mr. Zhenyong Liu commented:
&ldquo;In the first quarter of FY2024, we realized revenue of approximately $6.86 million with a profit of $0.40 million. During the reporting
period, domestic packaging paper suffered sluggish demand and prices. In addition, the increase in production capacity of the industry
peers, more intense competition from import of finished products and interest rate hikes had posed persistent pressure on the industry.
Despite these daunting challenges, China is actively launching various policies to simulate the economy and support enterprises, which
is believed to be effective in boosting investment and domestic demand, thereby improving the business environment of the packaging paper
industry. Looking forward, we will continue to optimize the raw material structure and minimize the purchase price to ensure production
efficiency and consistent quality. We also will explore new products and new markets with appropriate price adjustments to capture greater
market share. Meanwhile, we believe that together with the above measures, and better control of the inventory and working capital as
well as cash flow, we will make the company a healthy operation in the near future.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>First Quarter 2024
Unaudited Financial Results</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><I>Revenue</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">For the first quarter
of 2024, total revenue decreased by 65.32%, to&nbsp;approximately $6.86 million&nbsp;from&nbsp;approximately $19.79 million&nbsp;for the
same period of last year. This was mainly due to production suspension of corrugating medium paper (&ldquo;CMP&rdquo;) in January and
February of 2024, and production suspension of tissue paper products in the first quarter of 2024.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">The following table summarizes
revenue, volume and ASP by product for the first quarter of 2024 and 2023, respectively:</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from CMP, including both regular CMP and
light-Weight CMP, decreased by 65.04%, to&nbsp;approximately $6.83 million&nbsp;and accounted for 100% of total revenue for the first
quarter of 2024, compared to&nbsp;approximately $19.53 million, or 98.67% of total revenue for the same period of last year. The Company
sold 18,670 tonnes of CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$366/tonne in the first quarter of 2024, compared to 49,682&nbsp;tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$393/tonne
in the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 2; Options: NewSection; Value: 2 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid"><P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; text-align: center; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt"><!-- Field: Sequence; Type: Arabic; Name: PageNo -->2<!-- Field: /Sequence --></P></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Of the total CMP sales, revenue from regular CMP
decreased by 65.08%, to&nbsp;approximately $5.75 million for the first quarter of 2024, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $16.47
million for the same period of last year. The Company sold 15,640 tonnes of regular CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$368/tonne during the first
quarter of 2024, compared to 41,663 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$395/tonne for the same period of last year. Revenue from light-weight CMP
decreased by 64.83%, to&nbsp;approximately $1.08 million for the first quarter of 2024, compared to revenue of&nbsp;approximately $3.06
million for the same period of last year. The Company sold 3,030 tonnes of light-weight CMP at an ASP of&nbsp;$355/tonne for the first
quarter of 2024, compared to 8,019 tonnes at an ASP of&nbsp;$382/tonne for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Revenue from offset printing paper was $nil &nbsp;for
the first quarter of 2024 and 2023.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Revenue from tissue paper
products was $nil and $222,953 for the three months ended March 31, 2024 and 2023, respectively. Production of tissue paper products was
suspended during the first quarter of 2024.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Revenue generated from
selling face mask were $nil and $35,637 for the three months ended March 31, 2024 and 2023, respectively.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>Gross Profit (Loss)
and Gross Margin</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Total cost of sales decreased by 67.79%, to&nbsp;approximately
$6.46 million&nbsp;for the first quarter of 2024 from&nbsp;approximately $20.07 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year. This was
mainly due to the decrease in sales quantity and the decrease in the unit material costs of CMP.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">Total gross profit was&nbsp;approximately $0.40
million&nbsp;for the first quarter of 2024, compare to the gross loss of&nbsp;approximately $0.28 million&nbsp;for the same period of
last year as a result of factors described above. Overall gross profit margin was 5.81% for the first quarter of 2024, compared to gross
loss margin of 1.40% for the same period of last year. Gross profit (loss) margins for regular CMP, light-weight CMP, offset printing
paper, tissue paper products and face mask products were 5.68%, 3.32%, nil%, nil% and nil%, respectively, for the first quarter of 2024,
compared to 1.93%, 3.96%, nil%, -316.80% and -7.97%, respectively, for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"></P>

Administrative Expenses</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Selling, general and
administrative expenses (&ldquo;SG&amp;A&rdquo;) increased by 56.32%, to&nbsp;approximately $3.90 million&nbsp;for the first quarter of
2024 from&nbsp;approximately $2.50 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>Loss from Operations</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Loss from operations
was&nbsp;approximately $3.50 million&nbsp;for the first quarter of 2024, a decrease of 26.31%, from $2.77 million&nbsp;for the same period
of last year. Operating loss margin was 51.02% for the first quarter of 2024, compared to 14.01% for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>Net Loss</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Net loss was&nbsp;approximately
$3.75 million, or loss per share of $0.37 for the first quarter of 2024, compared to $2.73 million, or loss per share of $0.27 for the
same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><I>EBITDA</I></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">EBITDA was&nbsp;approximately
$-0.02 million&nbsp;for the first quarter of 2024, compared to&nbsp; $1.21 million&nbsp;for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Note 1: Non-GAAP Financial
Measures</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">In addition to our U.S.
GAAP results, this press release includes a discussion of EBITDA, a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by the Securities and Exchange
Commission (&ldquo;SEC&rdquo;). The Company defines EBITDA as net income before interest, income taxes, depreciation and amortization. EBITDA
is a key measure used by management to evaluate our results and make strategic decisions. Management believes this measure is useful to
investors because it is an indicator of operational performance. Because not all companies use identical calculations, the Company&rsquo;s presentation
of EBITDA may not be comparable to similarly titled measures of other companies, and should not be viewed as an alternative to measures
of financial performance or changes in cash flows calculated in accordance with the U.S. GAAP.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>Cash, Liquidity and
Financial Position</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left">As of&nbsp;March 31, 2024, the Company had cash
and bank balances, short-term debt (including bank loans, current portion of long-term loans from credit union and related party loans),
and long-term debt (including related party loans) of&nbsp;approximately $4.51 million,&nbsp;$9.69 million and&nbsp;$3.24 million, respectively,
compared to &nbsp;approximately $3.92&nbsp;million,&nbsp;$8.03&nbsp;million and&nbsp;$4.50 million, respectively, as of&nbsp;December
31, 2023.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

Net cash used in investing activities was&nbsp;approximately $0.01 million&nbsp;for the first quarter of 2024, compared to approximately

the first quarter of 2024, compared to approximately $2.56 for the same period of last year.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white"><B>About IT Tech Packaging,
Inc.</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">Founded in 1996, IT Tech
Packaging, Inc. is a leading manufacturer and distributor of diversified paper products and single-use face masks in&nbsp;North China.
Using recycled paper as its primary raw material (with the exception of its tissue paper products), ITP produces and distributes three
categories of paper products: corrugating medium paper, offset printing paper and tissue paper products. With production based in Baoding
and Xingtai in&nbsp;North China&rsquo;s&nbsp;Hebei Province, ITP is located strategically close to the&nbsp;Beijing&nbsp;and&nbsp;Tianjin&nbsp;region,
home to a growing base of industrial and manufacturing activities and one of the largest markets for paper products consumption in the
country. ITP has been listed on the NYSE American since&nbsp;December 2009. For more information, please visit:&nbsp;http://www.itpackaging.cn/.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: left; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>
